Fall 2017 Schedules 

Sorted by the following criteria in order:

Sorted by Priority Score, in increasing order.
Sorted by Average Duration, in increasing order.
Sorted by Average Start, in decreasing order.



Mandatory Courses:  [('CS 2124 LEC', 'CS 2124 LAB'), 'MG 2204']
Optional/Elective Courses:  ['BMS-A 1004 LAB', 'BMS-A 1004 LEC', 'BMS-B 1004 LAB', 'BMS-B 1004 LEC', 'CM 1004', 'CS 2204 LAB', 'CS 2204 LEC', 'MA 2224', 'MG 2004', 'MG 2104', 'MG 2304', 'PH 2033', 'PH 2131']
Minimum Number of Credits:  16

Each schedule contains all mandatory courses.  
Not all schedules contain each optional/elective course.  
Courses in parentheses are corequisites and must be taken together.  
Schedules may meet or exceed minimum number of credits.
